Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    a = ()
    c = ()
    n = len(lst)
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i, n):
            if ((lst[i] == lst[j]) and (i != j)):
                a += (j,)
            else:
                continue
    b = tuple(set(a))
    for i in b:
        c += (lst[i],)
    d = lst[::(- 1)]
    for j in range(len(c)):
        d.remove(c[j])
    e = d[::(- 1)]
    return e
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    sub_list = []
    for elem in lst:
        if (elem not in lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]):
            return lst
        elif (elem in lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]):
            sub_list += lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]
            sub_list.remove(elem)
            return(lst[: lst.index(elem)] + sub_list)
```

the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    ref_lsts = []
    for ref_i in lst:
        if (ref_i not in ref_lsts):
            ref_lsts.append(ref_i)
        elif False:
            pass
    lst = ref_lsts
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    sub_list = []
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    lst.sort()
    i = 0
    while (i < len(lst)):
        if (i == (len(lst) - 1)):
            break
        elif (lst[i] == lst[(i + 1)]):

        else:
            i += 1
    return lst
```

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    for i in range(len(lst) - 1, -1, -1):
        if lst[i] in lst[:i] + lst[i+1:]:
            lst.pop(i)
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new_lst = []
    if lst == []:
        return new_lst
    elif lst[0] in new_lst:
        return new_lst + remove_extras(lst[1:])
    else:
        new_lst.append(lst[0])
        return new_lst + remove_extras(lst[1:])
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    if lst == []:
        return []
    elif lst[-1] in lst[:-1]:
        return remove_extras(lst[:-1])
    else:
        return remove_extras(lst[:-1]) + [lst[-1]]
```

wrong_3_202.py
------------
User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- remove_extras
- lst
- new_lst
- i
- a
- h
- ele

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new_lst = [lst[0]]
    if (lst == []):
        return []
    for i in range(len(lst)):
        a = lst[i]
        for h in range(i, len(lst)):
            if (a != lst[h]):
                ele = lst[h]
                if (ele in new_lst):
                    continue
                new_lst.append(ele)
    return new_lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    i = 0
    while i < l:
        j = i + 1
        while j < l:
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
            else:
                j += 1
        i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    for i in range(l):
        for j in range((i + 1), l):
```

the corrected code is incorrect

Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    i = 0
    while i < l:
        j = i + 1
        while j < l:
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
            else:
                j += 1
        i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
```
```python
    lst.reverse()
```
```python
    for i in lst:
```
```python
        n = len(lst)
```
```python
        counter = 1
        number_of_appearance = 0
        while (counter <= n):
            if (i == lst[(counter - 1)]):
                counter += 1
                number_of_appearance += 1
            else:
                counter += 1
        while (number_of_appearance != 1):
            lst.remove(i)
            number_of_appearance -= 1
    lst.reverse()
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    i = 0
    while i < l:
        j = i + 1
        while j < l:
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
            else:
                j += 1
        i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
        if (lst[i] in lst[(i + 1):]):
            ref_ext = lst[(i + 1):]
            ref_ext.remove(lst[i])
            lst = (lst[:(i + 1)] + ref_ext)
        else:
            i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    i = 0
```
```python
    new = []
    while (i < len(lst)):

        new += [curr]

            if (ele == curr):

            new += [ele]
        lst = new.copy()
        new = []
        i += 1
    lst.reverse()
    return lst
```

```python
        counter += 1
```
```python
    return result
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    keep = []
    remove = []
    for i in lst:
        if (i not in keep):
            keep.append(i)
        else:

    return lst
```

```python
    keep = []
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    i = 0
    while (i < len(lst)):
        if (lst[i] in lst[(i + 1):]):
            ref_ext = lst[(i + 1):]
            ref_ext.remove(lst[i])
            lst = (lst[:(i + 1)] + ref_ext)
        else:
            i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    count = lst.copy()
    rev_lst = lst.copy()
    rev_lst.reverse()
    ori_len = len(lst)
    for i in range(ori_len):
        if (rev_lst[i] in rev_lst[(i + 1):]):
            count.pop(((ori_len - i) - 1))
    return count
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    for i in lst:
        remove_multiple(i, lst)
    return lst

def remove_multiple(n, lst):
    if lst.count(n) == 1:
        return lst
    else:
        lst.reverse()
        lst.remove(n)
        lst.reverse()
        return remove_multiple(n, lst)
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    def position(i):
        n = len(lst)
        for j in range(n):
            if (lst[j] == i):
                return j
    def helper(start, i):
        for k in lst[start:]:
            if (k == i):
                lst.remove(k)
        else:
            pass
    if (lst == []):
        return[]
    new_lst = [lst[0]]
    for i in range(len(lst)):
        index = position(i)
        helper((index + 1), i)
    return lst
```

the corrected code is incorrect

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new_lst = []
    for i in lst:
        if i not in new_lst:
            new_lst.append(i)
    return new_lst
```

```python
    sub_list = []
    for elem in lst:
        if (elem not in lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]):
            return lst
        elif (elem in lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]):
            sub_list += lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]
            while (elem in sub_list):
                sub_list.remove(elem)
            return(lst[:(lst.index(elem) + 1)] + sub_list)
```
